


---

Question: What is century?
Answer: century is A period of 100 consecutive years; often specifically a numbered period with conventional start and end dates, e.g., the twentieth century, which stretches from (strictly) 1901 through 2000, or (informally) 1900 through 1999. The first century AD was from 1 to 100..

Question: What is roads?
Answer: roads is A way used for travelling between places, originally one wide enough to allow foot passengers and horses to travel, now (US) usually one surfaced with asphalt or concrete and designed to accommodate many vehicles travelling in both directions. In the UK both senses are heard: a country road is the same as a country lane..

Answer: Variables in JavaScript store data values. You can declare them with let, const, or var.

Q: What does flowering mean?
A: flowering is To put forth blooms..

---

Q: What does subfamily mean?
A: subfamily is A taxonomic category ranking between a family and a genus; formerly called a tribe.

---

Q: What does tribe mean?
A: tribe is A socially, ethnically, or politically cohesive group of people..

---

Q: What does plant mean?
A: plant is An organism that is not an animal, especially an organism capable of photosynthesis. Typically a small or herbaceous organism of this kind, rather than a tree..

---

Q: What does family mean?
A: family is A group of people who are closely related to one another (by blood, marriage or adoption); kin; for example, a set of parents and their children; an immediate family..

---

Q: What does late mean?
A: late is A shift (scheduled work period) that takes place late in the day or at night..

---

Q: What does county mean?
A: county is The land ruled by a count or a countess..

---

Q: What does north mean?
A: north is One of the four major compass points, specifically 0°, directed toward the North Pole, and conventionally upwards on a map, abbreviated as N..

---

Q: What does junction mean?
A: junction is The act of joining, or the state of being joined..

---

Q: What does population mean?
A: population is The people living within a political or geographical boundary..

---

Q: What does townland mean?
A: townland is A geographical unit of land smaller than a parish..

---

Q: What does making mean?
A: making is The act of forming, causing, or constituting; workmanship; construction..

---

Q: What does century mean?
A: century is A period of 100 consecutive years; often specifically a numbered period with conventional start and end dates, e.g., the twentieth century, which stretches from (strictly) 1901 through 2000, or (informally) 1900 through 1999. The first century AD was from 1 to 100..

---

Q: What does largest mean?
A: largest is Of considerable or relatively great size or extent..

---

Q: What does within mean?
A: within is In the context of which the present document or ruling is made..

---

Q: What does roads mean?
A: roads is A way used for travelling between places, originally one wide enough to allow foot passengers and horses to travel, now (US) usually one surfaced with asphalt or concrete and designed to accommodate many vehicles travelling in both directions. In the UK both senses are heard: a country road is the same as a country lane..

---

Q: What does beetle mean?
A: beetle is A small car, the Volkswagen Beetle (original version made 1938–2003, similar models made 1997–2010 and since 2011).

---

Q: What does brazil mean?
A: brazil is A red-orange dye obtained from brazil wood..

---

Q: What does music mean?
A: music is A series of sounds organized in time, employing melody, harmony, tempo etc. usually to convey a mood..

---

Q: What does electronic mean?
A: electronic is : Of or pertaining to an electron or electrons..

---

Q: What does musician mean?
A: musician is A composer, conductor, or performer of music; specifically, a person who sings and/or plays a musical instrument as a hobby, an occupation, or a profession..

---

Q: What does range mean?
A: range is A line or series of mountains, buildings, etc..

---

Q: What does plays mean?
A: plays is Activity for amusement only, especially among the young..

Answer: century is A period of 100 consecutive years; often specifically a numbered period with conventional start and end dates, e.g., the twentieth century, which stretches from (strictly) 1901 through 2000, or (informally) 1900 through 1999. The first century AD was from 1 to 100..

---

Question: What is region?
Answer: region is Any considerable and connected part of a space or surface; specifically, a tract of land or sea of considerable but indefinite extent; a country; a district; in a broad sense, a place without special reference to location or extent but viewed as an entity for geographical, social or cultural reasons..

Question: Define roads.
Answer: A way used for travelling between places, originally one wide enough to allow foot passengers and horses to travel, now (US) usually one surfaced with asphalt or concrete and designed to accommodate many vehicles travelling in both directions. In the UK both senses are heard: a country road is the same as a country lane.

Continue: In theoretical physics, a roton is an elementary excitation, or quasiparticle, seen in superfluid helium-4 and Bose–Einstein condensates with long-range dipolar interactions or spin-orbit coupling. → The dispersion relation of elementary excitations in this superfluid shows a linear increase from the origin, but exhibits first a maximum and then a minimum in energy as the momentum increases. Excitations with momenta in the linear region are called phonons; those with momenta close to the minimum are called rotons.

Continue: Mounted search and rescue (MSAR) is a specialty within search and rescue (SAR), using horses as search partners and for transportation to search for missing persons. SAR responders on horseback are primarily a search resource, but also can provide off-road logistics support and transportation. → Mounted SAR responders can in some terrains move faster on the ground than a human on foot, can transport more equipment, and may be physically less exhausted than a SAR responder performing the same task on foot. Mounted SAR responders typically have longer initial response times than groundpounder SAR resources, due to the time required to pick up trailer, horse(s), and perhaps also water, feed, and equipment.

Continue: In theoretical physics, a roton is an elementary excitation, or quasiparticle, seen in superfluid helium-4 and Bose–Einstein condensates with long-range dipolar interactions or spin-orbit coupling. The dispersion relation of elementary excitations in this superfluid shows a linear increase from the origin, but exhibits first a maximum and then a minimum in energy as the momentum increases. → Excitations with momenta in the linear region are called phonons; those with momenta close to the minimum are called rotons. Excitations with momenta near the maximum are called maxons.

Continue: Mounted search and rescue (MSAR) is a specialty within search and rescue (SAR), using horses as search partners and for transportation to search for missing persons. → SAR responders on horseback are primarily a search resource, but also can provide off-road logistics support and transportation. Mounted SAR responders can in some terrains move faster on the ground than a human on foot, can transport more equipment, and may be physically less exhausted than a SAR responder performing the same task on foot.

Question: Define roads.
Answer: A way used for travelling between places, originally one wide enough to allow foot passengers and horses to travel, now (US) usually one surfaced with asphalt or concrete and designed to accommodate many vehicles travelling in both directions. In the UK both senses are heard: a country road is the same as a country lane.
